 On August 21, the Governor sent back the files related to the appointment of the Lokayukta to the government for the third time, saying that in view of the Supreme Court's order passed on July 23, the Chief Justice of the Chief Minister of Allahabad High Court and the Leader of the State Legislative Assembly, the opposition consulted and After concurrence, propose one name for appointment of new Lokayukta
 nik ne file teesri baar lautaate hue 10 prishthon kaa patr likhaa tha, jisamen unhone mukhya nyaayadhish chandrachud ke patron kaa zikr kiya tha, jisamen unhone kaha tha, ‘‘chaar main se teen patron main maine nyaayamurti rabindra singh kii niyukti se asahmat hone ke kaaran bataaye the
 i want to clarify those reasons by reiterating that i do not agree with the appointment of Ravindra Singh to the post of Lokayukta
 ’’ The Governor referred to another letter from Justice Chandrachud, in which he mentioned the presence of Justice Ravindra Singh along with senior government minister Shivpal Singh Yadav at a public function, in the public eye towards a particular party
 There is a doubt that the person having an inclination will be able to execute the responsibility of the Lokayukta in a fair manner
 ucchtam nyaayalay ne gat 23 july ko rajya sarkaar se kaha tha ki vah lokayukta pad par niyukti ke liye 22 agast tak koi naam sujhaaye jiske baad sarkaar ne rabindra singh yadav kaa naam tay karke usase sambandhit file paanch agast ko pehali baar rajbhavan ko bheji thi
 The comments pradesh main march 2012 main akhilesh yadav sarkaar ke gathan ke baad pradesh main lokayukta ke kaarykaal ko chah se badhaakar aath saal karne kii baat kahi gai thi
 The current Lokayukta NK Mehrotra has been in this position for nine years
 rajyapal ne file waapas bhejte hue spasht kar diya tha ki mukhyamantri, elahabaad ucch nyaayalay ke mukhya nyaayadhish evam rajya vidhansabha ke netaa vipaksh kii chayan samiti kii baithak main naam tay hone ke baad hi vah file par apni manjuuri denge
 Governor Naik said that the government has sent for the fourth time on Saturday in a file that recommended the reappointment of retired Justice Ravindra Singh Yadav
 unhone bataaya ki sarkaar ne kaha he ki is pad par niyukti ke liye mukhyamantri or netaa pratipaksh kii do sadasyeey chayan samiti he or donon ke bich is sambandh main baithak ho chuki he
 The Governor said that in the file from Chief Minister Akhilesh, it has been said that the advice of the Chief Justice of the High Court has also been taken regarding the appointment of Lokayukta
 magar vah chayan prakriya par badhyakaari nahin he
 Naik said that he is taking judicial opinion on various aspects of the government's recommendation and will take whatever decision is taken soon
 netaa pratipaksh swami prasad maury kaa kahana he ki chayan samiti main mukhya nyaayadhish bhi sadsy hai or kisi ek naam kii sanstuti ke liye teenon kii sahmati jaruri he
 Maurya said, "in the discussion with me, the Chief Minister said that the Chief Justice of Allahabad High Court Justice DY Chandrachud has also been consulted in this regard and he has given his recommendation
" ’’ He said that 5-6 meetings were held in this regard, but none included the Chief Justice
 rajyapal ne 21 agast ko lokayukta kii niyukti sambandhi filon ko teesri baar sarkaar ko waapas bhejte hue kaha tha ki ucchtam nyaayalay ke gat 23 july ko paarit aadesh ke maddenjar mukhyamantri elahabaad ucch nyaayalay ke mukhya nyaayadhish evam rajya vidhansabha ke netaa vipaksh aapasi vichaar-vimarsh evam sahmati ke baad koi ek naam nae lokayukta kii niyukti ke liye prastaavit karen
 Naik wrote a 10-page letter returning the file for the third time, referring to the letters of Chief Justice Chandrachud, in which he said, "in three out of four letters i disagreed with the appointment of Justice Ravindra Singh
 Were told main un kaarnon ko doharaate hue spasht kahana chahta hum ki main lokayukta pad par rabindra singh kii niyukti se sahamat nahin hum
 '' rajyapal ne nyaayamurti chandrachud ke ek or patr kaa zikr kiya tha, jisamen unhone ek saarvajanik kaarykram main sarkaar ke varisht mantri shivpal singh yadav ke saath nyaayamurti rabindra singh ke upasthit rahane kaa ullekh karte hue kaha tha ki janata kii nigaah main kisi dal vishesh ke prati jhukaav rakhane vaala vyakti lokayukta ke daayitv kaa nishpaksh tareeke se nishpaadan kar paayegaa, isamen andeh he
 On July 23, the Supreme Court had asked the state government to suggest a name for appointment to the post of Lokayukta till August 22, after which the government decided the name of Ravindra Singh Yadav and sent the file related to it to Raj Bhavan for the first time on August 5
 tippaniyan After the formation of Akhilesh Yadav government in the state in March 2012, it was said that the Lokayukta's tenure in the state should be increased from six to eight years
 maujuuda lokayukta enke mehrotra nau saal se is pad par hai
 While sending the file back, the Governor made it clear that the Chief Minister, Chief Justice of Allahabad High Court and the Leader of the State Legislative Assembly will give their approval on the file only after the name is decided in the meeting of the selection committee of the opposition

 vaise to yah raqam badi nahin he lekin khilaadiyon ko iskaa malaal bhi nahin
 But it is a matter of concern that the picture of tomorrow of this team is not very clear
 zyaadaatar khilaadiyon ke liye sponcer or naukari kii talash jari he
 These junior players have fulfilled their responsibility by maintaining history on the field of hockey
 hockey india in sabhi khilaadiyon or saport staff ke karname se prabhavit to he magar isse zyada paise de paanaa unke bas main nahin
 The corporate world is currently unable to hear the echoes of this victory and is pretending to be uninformed
 agar khilaadiyon kii haalat or zarurat ko sunen to or bura lag saktaa he
 Ranchi's superhero goalkeeper Bigan Soy says, "I will spend whatever money is received to build a house
" isse puraa ghar to nahin ban paaegaa, lekin chalegaa
 i am very happy ' Vandana Kataria, who works in Railways, is in better condition than Bigan Soy
 unke pita ke paas public sector main naukari he
 Vandana says, 'she will give the money to the family members
 unhen zarurat he
 Will work for them
 
 
 lekin unhen ummid he ki is jeet se corporate jagat or spancer unki madad ke liye zarur aage aaenge
 In the past too, the courage of these girls, who find a different motivation for themselves, is not broken
 ye sab isi ummid se khelti hai ki hockey kii tasviir ek din zarur badalegi
 Rani Rampal, who became the Player of the Tournament in the World Cup, says
 
 
 'mujhe lagata he ki ye tasviir zarur badalegi
 This picture must be changed
 ' MN Poonamma of Karnataka does not have a job but she understands the condition of hockey and its reason
 vah kahati hai, 'yah to pehla kadam he
 We will work harder in the upcoming tournament
 logon ko hamase ummid bandhi he or ham unhen karke dikhaaenge
 ' vandana kataaria corporate world se apil karti hai ki unki baat se nahin unke khel ko dekhakar corporate world ko aage aana chahie
 Many players in the team do not have jobs
 sabko naukari kii zarurat he
 Narendra Batra, the General Secretary of Hockey India, says that corporate houses make claims but pull back in time for help
 narendra batra kaa kahana he ki kuch corporate houseej ko chhod den to baaki lip sarvice karte hai
 Not many corporates come forward for these games
 rajya sarkaar or corporate jagat ko aage aana chahie
 While hockey journalist k Arumugam considers the hockey system responsible for all this
 vah kehete hai ki agar aap saal main ek yaa do toornament karoge to corporate aapaki kaise madad karegaa
 You have to do something completely different like the Indian Badminton League
 aap corporate world ke liye sochenge tabhi ve aapaki madad kar paaenge
 The comments in sabake bich coach narendra singh saini yaa mahila team ke coach rahe emke kowshik itnaa zarur kehete hai ki team ke paas achche junior khilaadi hai or inke aadhaar par agar is maukey kaa faaydaa uthaaya jaae to hockey kii buland imaarat khadi kii ja sakati he
 The use of the four-day moonlight proverb may be too much for hockey victories and their reception, but if the hockey system and the corporate world did not use it properly, then the importance of this win can also become history

 In Bastar district of Chhattisgarh, Naxalites stopped the work of road construction
 in ilaakon main barish ke pehle nirmaan kaary ko purna kar lene kaa lakshya, do saal pehle hi nirdhaarit kar diya gaya tha
 The police and central security forces also exerted their full force to accomplish the goal
 lekin bade naksali hamalon ke chalate sarkaar ke armaanon par pani phir gaya he
 Naxalites have succeeded in stopping the pace of construction work
 bastar main do darjan se zyada sadakon main ab naa to majdoor nazar aate he or naa hi sarkari afasar , thekedaar or suraksha karmi
 In fact, police and central security forces have been withdrawn from all roads
 isse vahaan nirmaan kaary thapp pad gaya he 
 CRPF has returned from the streets after the Sukma attack
 Construction of 25 roads in Bastar has been suspended in half following the attack on CRPF personnel in Burukapal, Barracksukama
 in sadakon par 6 maheene ke liye kaam band kar diya gaya he
 In all seven districts of Bastar, contractors and laborers have also surrendered their goods from road construction sites due to the fear of Maoist attack
 in ilaakon main aazaadee ke baad se kabhi bhi sadake nahin bani thi
 In the time of eastern Madhya Pradesh, only raw roads were built in most areas
 | in sadakon kii marammat bhi kabhi kabhaar hi hui
 The situation remained the same after the formation of the state of Chhattisgarh in 2001
 pehle congress or uske baadamukhyamantri raman singhke kaarykaal ke das saalon main bhi in sadakon kii haalat jas kii tas bani rahi
 Because the Naxalites are completely dominating in these areas
 bijepi jab teesri baar satta main ai to phir bastar main nirmaan ke kaaryon ne jor pakadana shuru kar liya
 Police Housing Corporation, especially in the Naxalite affected areas, took responsibility for the road construction work, which started changing the picture of the village
 jangal ke bhitari raaston ke bajaaye gramin pakki sadakon par chahalkadami karne lage
 Movement in the village also started
 yatri bas, jeep , car or duusare vaahanon kii bhi awajahi shuru ho gai
 At the same time vehicles of police and security forces also started running on these roads
 bas naksaliyon ko yahi akharane laga
 The vehicles of the police and security forces became the eyes of their eyes
 maovadiyon ke hausale buland , gramin hue maayusnaksaliyon ne aam force ke bajaaye sadak nirmaan kii suraksha main lagi CRPF team ko nishaanaa bananaa shuru kar diya
 Earlier this year, on March 11 in Sukma, CRPF squad attacked and targeted 11 soldiers
 iske baad 24 april ko sukama main hi CRPF ke 25 jawan naksali hamale main shahid ho gaye the
 Both events brought the state and the central government to a standstill
 sukhmaake burkapal main hue hamale ke baad CRPF ke tatkaaleen dijipi ' sudhir lakhatkia ' ne sadak nirmaan nahin karne or force ko hatane kaa nirdesh de diya tha
 After which the Force returned to their barracks
 tab se hi tamaam ilaakon main sadak nirmaan kaa puraa kaam thapp padaa hua he
